PROC
PROC_DebugBook_AddConditionalEntries((CHARACTER)_Var1, (CHARACTER)_Var1, (CHARACTER)_Var1, (CHARACTER)_Var1, (CHARACTER)_Var1)
AND
DB_InRegion(_Var1, S_IRN_IronThrone_SUB_559c1c28-b3b7-49fb-8897-36272a2d6f33, _Var1, _Var1, _Var1)
THEN
DB_DebugBookEntry_Temp("Wyll", "Saving Ravengard Options", "Go to Ravengard", "Wyll_IRN_GotoRavengard", 1);
DB_DebugBookEntry_Temp("Wyll", "Saving Ravengard Options", "Escape and save Ravengard", "Wyll_IRN_SaveRavengard", 1);
DB_DebugBookEntry_Temp("Wyll", "Saving Ravengard Options", "Escape and don't save Ravengard", "Wyll_IRN_DontSaveRavengard", 1);
DB_DebugBookEntry_Temp("Wyll", "Saving Ravengard Options", "Ravengard present", "Wyll_IRN_RavengardPresent", 0);
DB_DebugBookEntry_Temp("Wyll", "Saving Ravengard Options", "Ravengard absent", "Wyll_IRN_RavengardAbsent", 0);
DB_DebugBookEntry_Temp("Wyll", "Saving Ravengard Options", "Mizora friendly", "Wyll_Act3_MizoraFriendly", 0);
DB_DebugBookEntry_Temp("Wyll", "Saving Ravengard Options", "Mizora enemy ", "Wyll_Act3_MizoraEnemy", 0);

THEN
PROC_TeleportPartiesTo(S_IRN_Debug_TeleportToRavengard_9a5c2820-1427-4e82-b9dd-a15b7e0a18ab, "");

PROC
PROC_DebugBook_Event("Wyll_IRN_SaveRavengard", _, _, _, _)
AND
GetFlag(IRN_IronThrone_State_IndividualPrisonerEscaped_a09945e7-6436-40e7-908e-22a699ef296e, S_GLO_Ravengard_f6620372-ebd0-4511-a39d-8c2d4ad03f03, 0, _, _)
THEN
SetFlag(IRN_IronThrone_State_IndividualPrisonerEscaped_a09945e7-6436-40e7-908e-22a699ef296e, S_GLO_Ravengard_f6620372-ebd0-4511-a39d-8c2d4ad03f03);

PROC
PROC_DebugBook_Event("Wyll_IRN_SaveRavengard", _, (CHARACTER)_, (CHARACTER)_, (CHARACTER)_)
THEN
PROC_TeleportPartiesTo(S_IRN_Debug_StartCountdownPos_66dd9741-ba35-4e0f-bc97-b0e2f0f301c0, "");
TimerLaunch("Wyll_IRN_SaveRavengard_DialogDelay", 1000);

IF
TimerFinished("Wyll_IRN_SaveRavengard_DialogDelay", _, _, _, _)
THEN
PROC_State_Progress(S_GLO_IronThrone_StateProgressHelper_954459bd-8fc3-4c16-8224-0343cacb1a01, "IRN_IronThrone", "CountdownFinished");

PROC
PROC_DebugBook_Event("Wyll_IRN_DontSaveRavengard", _, (CHARACTER)_, (CHARACTER)_, (CHARACTER)_)
THEN
PROC_TeleportPartiesTo(S_IRN_Debug_StartCountdownPos_66dd9741-ba35-4e0f-bc97-b0e2f0f301c0, "");
ClearFlag(IRN_IronThrone_State_IndividualPrisonerEscaped_a09945e7-6436-40e7-908e-22a699ef296e, S_GLO_Ravengard_f6620372-ebd0-4511-a39d-8c2d4ad03f03);
PROC_SetOnStage(S_GLO_Ravengard_f6620372-ebd0-4511-a39d-8c2d4ad03f03, 0);
PROC_State_Progress(S_GLO_IronThrone_StateProgressHelper_954459bd-8fc3-4c16-8224-0343cacb1a01, "IRN_IronThrone", "CountdownFinished");

THEN

DB_WYR_RaphaelTango_PartOfScene(S_GLO_GithKnight_2adce2df-0799-49dc-b867-ba7ca21e9aea);

PROC_Debug_ORI_Laezel_ResetVossAct3State();
PROC_SetOnStage(S_GLO_GithKnight_2adce2df-0799-49dc-b867-ba7ca21e9aea, 1);
DB_Dialogs(S_GLO_GithKnight_2adce2df-0799-49dc-b867-ba7ca21e9aea, WYR_RaphaelTango_Voss_140953a8-5d79-c6d0-d691-52694b875bc2);
SetFlag(ORI_Laezel_State_BetrayedByVlaakith_175d8487-99dc-4009-9b45-6e9f29708cd7);
SetFlag(ORI_Laezel_State_MetVossInAct2_26563f96-bf5a-4895-b63b-036c7571bbbc);
SetFlag(ORI_Laezel_State_AgreedWithVossInAct2_63f1a107-a2af-46ec-ac49-a10d0166ac2e);
